  * grade_story_0.txt (grade=8.1)
    The Pattern Recognition Center is vividly established as a sterile, logical environment, with the stained glass lamp providing excellent visual contrast that reinforces thematic elements. The mandatory naptime creates a distinctive atmosphere that enhances tension. The facility feels like a real place with its own rules and aesthetics, though more sensory details beyond visual elements would have strengthened immersion.

  * grade_story_104.txt (grade=8.5)

The contrast between the mundane setting (a public restroom) and the mystical elements creates effective juxtaposition that enhances the story's themes.
